<p style="text-align: center;"><em>Payloads internal name and TimeDateStamp</em></p>
<h1>Final notes</h1>
<p>BumbleBee threat actors are not the first to change the initial access method from malicious office documents to malicious ISO image files. The ISO image file abuse was also seen a few years ago, but in recent months, we have observed an increase in “ISO campaigns.”</p>
<p>Different threat actors abuse ISO image files to deliver their payloads. For example, BazarISO deploys Bazarloader, and IcedID started to use ISO image files instead of MalDocs like in the two examples below.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" width="1090" height="257" class="wp-image-42774 aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201090%20257'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email Description automatically generated" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22.png 1090w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-300x71.png 300w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-1024x241.png 1024w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-768x181.png 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 1090px) 100vw, 1090px" data-lazy-src="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22.png" /><noscript><img loading="lazy" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1090" height="257" class="wp-image-42774 aligncenter" src="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22.png" alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email Description automatically generated" srcset="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22.png 1090w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-300x71.png 300w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-1024x241.png 1024w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-email-22-768x181.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1090px) 100vw, 1090px" /></noscript></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em>Documents-17.iso (Bazarloader)</em></p>
<p><img decoding="async" width="980" height="254" class="wp-image-42775 aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20980%20254'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Graphical user interface, text, application Description automatically generated" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38.png 980w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38-300x78.png 300w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38-768x199.png 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 980px) 100vw, 980px" data-lazy-src="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38.png" /><noscript><img loading="lazy" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="980" height="254" class="wp-image-42775 aligncenter" src="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38.png" alt="Graphical user interface, text, application Description automatically generated" srcset="https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38.png 980w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38-300x78.png 300w, https://www.cynet.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/graphical-user-interface-text-application-descr-38-768x199.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 980px) 100vw, 980px" /></noscript></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em> Invoice_pdf_1.iso (IcedID)</em></p>
<p>In most of the cases, we’ve seen that during different IR cases, the campaigns escalated to full-blown ransomware attacks. We believe that IAB groups work and collaborate with ransomware affiliates like CONTI, LockBit, AvosLocker, and more. For example, we observed an IcedID infection that leads to CONTI ransomware attack (Shelob Moonlight).</p>
<p>The Orion team is constantly monitoring BumbleBee and the IAB group&#8217;s activities closely and analyzing them to better understand their motivation. As we learn more, we will publish our findings and artifacts to share additional insights for BumbleBee infection to ransomware post-attack chain.</p>
<p>We&#8217;re expecting to see more malware campaigns that will use the ISO delivery method in the near future. So, stay vigilant.</p>
<p>As a final note, we’d like to share these indicators of compromise with you.</p>

function forceZoomInfoShortening() {
  // prevent multiple runs
  if (window.__zoominfo_reran) return;
  window.__zoominfo_reran = true;

  // 1️⃣ DOM mutation (ZoomInfo listens to this)
  document.dispatchEvent(new Event("DOMContentLoaded", { bubbles: true }));
  window.dispatchEvent(new Event("load"));

  // 2️⃣ Hard re-append ZoomInfo script (MOST RELIABLE)
  setTimeout(function () {
    var ziScript = document.querySelector('script[src*="zoominfo"]');
    if (!ziScript) return;

    var clone = ziScript.cloneNode(true);
    ziScript.parentNode.removeChild(ziScript);
    document.head.appendChild(clone);
  }, 300);
}

									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}

/* entrance animation js*/

	/**
	 * is element in viewport
	 */
    function ueIsElementInViewport(objElement) {
	  
	  if(document.body.scrollHeight <= (window.innerHeight + 30) )
		return(true);	

      var elementTop = objElement.offset().top;
      var elementBottom = elementTop + objElement.outerHeight();

      var viewportTop = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
      var viewportBottom = viewportTop + jQuery(window).height();

      return (elementBottom > viewportTop && elementTop < viewportBottom);
	}

			
  //start the animation - add animation class
  function ueStartEntranceAnimation(objElement, step, classItem, order){

    var time = 0;

    if(!step)
    	var step = 100;

    var objItems = objElement.find("."+classItem).not(".uc-entrance-animate");

    var numItems = objItems.length;

    if(numItems == 0)
    	return(false);

    var maxTime = (numItems-1) * step;

    objItems.each(function(index, item){
	  
   	  var timeoutTime = time;
   	  if(order == "up")
   	  	timeoutTime = maxTime - time;

      var objItem = jQuery(item);

      setTimeout(function(){

            objItem.addClass("uc-entrance-animate");

      },timeoutTime);

      time += step;

    });
  }

    //check and add animation
    function ueCheckEntranceAnimation(objElement, step, classItem, order){

        var isStarted = objElement.data("ue_entrance_animation_started");

        if(isStarted === true)
        	return(false);

      	var isInside = ueIsElementInViewport(objElement);

        if(isInside == false)
          return(false);

        ueStartEntranceAnimation(objElement, step, classItem, order);

        objElement.data("ue_entrance_animation_started", true);
  }

			
jQuery(document).ready(function(){

  
  function initUEEntranceAnimation(){

	  var objElement = jQuery("#uc_post_grid_elementor_1fd84d74");

	  if(objElement.length == 0)
	  	 return(false);

	   if(typeof ueCheckEntranceAnimation == "undefined"){
	      return(false);
	   }

	    ueCheckEntranceAnimation(objElement, 100,"ue-item", "down");

	    jQuery(window).on("scroll", function(){
	    	ueCheckEntranceAnimation(objElement, 100, "ue-item", "down")
	    });
		
	    objElement.on("uc_ajax_refreshed", function(event, params){
				        
			objElement.removeData("ue_entrance_animation_started");
			
			if(params.isLoadMore && params.isLoadMore === true){
				
				ueStartEntranceAnimation(objElement, 100, "ue-item", "down");
				
				return(true);
			}
						
	    	ueCheckEntranceAnimation(objElement, 100, "ue-item", "down")
	    });

	return(true);
  }

  var isInited = initUEEntranceAnimation();

  if(isInited == false)
	  jQuery(document).on("elementor/popup/show", initUEEntranceAnimation);

});
